#Category only allowed for all china
#Category visible when PRC_coalition_government focus is completed for PRC
#Category visible when CHI_join_the_republican_government focus is completed for warlord

#Variables and flags and targets to know about
#Event target WTT_current_china_leader
#State variable for amount Support Points gained: state_political_support_value
#State flag: majority_political_platform_<TAG> for whoever has majority in the state
#Country flag: wtt_political_struggle for all countries involved in the struggle

#Variables:
#days_remove = global.days_add_support?1337 #DAYS_UNTIL_SUPPORRT_IN_STATE_IS_ADDED
#days_remove = global.days_remove_support?1337 #DAYS_UNTIL_REMOVE_SUPPORT


@PRC_CELL_SET_UP_AI_FACTOR = 100
@PRC_CELL_SET_UP_AI_FACTOR_2 = 20
@PRC_CELL_DECISIONS_COST = 20
@PRC_CELL_SEND_EQ_COST_TRIGGER = 499
@PRC_CELL_SEND_EQ_COST_TRIGGER_EFFECT = -500


PRC_dcat_frontline_behind_enemy_line = {
	
	PRC_uprise_in_states = {
		allowed = { original_tag = PRC }
		icon = revolt
		visible = {
			has_war_with = CHI
			any_state = { has_state_flag = KMT_PRC_state_has_guerrilla_cell }
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				any_state = {
					is_controlled_by = CHI
					check_variable = { PRC_state_guerrilla_cell_strength > 49 }
				}
				add = 1000
			}
		}
		
		cost = 0
		
		days_remove = 2
		days_re_enable = 90
		
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = PRC_jmcij_flag }}
				set_country_flag = PRC_jmcij_flag
				division_template = {
					name = "Jenmin Ch'iichun"	
					priority = 0
					regiments = { 
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 } 
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 } 
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 } 
					}
					is_locked = yes
				}
			}
		}
		
		available = {
			any_state = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = PRC_guerrilla_cell_requirement20_tt
					check_variable = { THIS.PRC_state_guerrilla_cell_strength > 19 }
				}
				CONTROLLER = {
					OR = {
						tag = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
						is_in_faction_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
						is_subject_of = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
					}
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_uprise_in_states_tt
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					CONTROLLER = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								OR = {
									tag = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
									is_in_faction_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
									is_subject_of = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
								}
								has_war_with = ROOT
							}
							tag = ROOT
						}
					}
					check_variable = { PRC_state_guerrilla_cell_strength > 19 }
				}
				PRC_guerrilla_civil_war_uprise = yes
				CONTROLLER = { country_event = { id = prc.309 }}
			}
		}
	}
}

@PRC_PACIFY_CELL_AI_BASE_FACTOR = 1000
@PRC_PACIFY_EQ_COST_TRIGGER = 99
@PRC_PACIFY_EQ_COST_EFFECT = -100
@PRC_PACIFY_CELL_DECISIONS_COST = 100

PRC_dcat_pacify_enemy_guerrilla_cell = {
	
	PRC_pacify_prc_cell = {
		icon = generic_scorched_earth
		
		highlight_states = {
		}
		
		visible = {
			controls_state = FROM
			FROM = {
				has_state_flag = KMT_PRC_state_cell_detected
			}
		}
		
		state_target = yes
		
		target_array = global.KMT_greater_china_region_states
		
		available = {
			FROM = {
				controller = { tag = ROOT }
				ROOT = {
					OR = {
						divisions_in_state = {
							state = PREV
							size > 1
						}
						has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > @PRC_PACIFY_EQ_COST_TRIGGER }
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			base = @PRC_PACIFY_CELL_AI_BASE_FACTOR
			modifier = {
				add = FROM.PRC_state_estimated_cell_strength
				FROM = { has_state_flag = KMT_PRC_state_cell_detected }
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					check_variable = { PRC_state_estimated_cell_strength > 5 }
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					check_variable = { PRC_state_estimated_cell_strength > 9 }
				}
				factor = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					check_variable = { PRC_state_estimated_cell_strength > 19 }
				}
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					check_variable = { PRC_state_estimated_cell_strength > 29 }
				}
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					check_variable = { PRC_state_estimated_cell_strength > 39 }
				}
				factor = 1000
			}
		}

		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 0

		cost = @PRC_PACIFY_CELL_DECISIONS_COST
		
		modifier = {
		}
		
		cancel_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					controller = { tag = ROOT }
					owner = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					has_state_flag = KMT_PRC_state_cell_detected
				}
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = @PRC_PACIFY_EQ_COST_EFFECT }
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				FROM = {
					save_global_event_target_as = PRC_temp_sweep_decision_target_state
				}
				PRC = { country_event = { id = prc.160 }}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						has_state_flag = KMT_PRC_state_has_guerrilla_cell
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					set_temp_variable = { PRC_max_pacify_score = PRC_state_estimated_cell_strength }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { PRC_max_pacify_score > 20 }}
						set_temp_variable = { PRC_max_pacify_score = 20 }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { var = PRC_state_guerrilla_cell_strength value = PRC_max_pacify_score }
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { PRC_state_guerrilla_cell_strength < 1 }
						}
						clr_state_flag = KMT_PRC_state_has_guerrilla_cell
					}
					clr_state_flag = KMT_PRC_state_cell_detected
					custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_estimated_cell_str_tt
					custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_sweep_target_state_cell_tt
				}
			}
		}
	}

@PRC_chinese_sweep_EQ_COST_TRIGGER = 149
@PRC_chinese_sweep_EQ_COST_EFFECT = -150
@PRC_chinese_sweep_CELL_AI_BASE_FACTOR = 1000
@PRC_chinese_sweep_CELL_DECISIONS_COST = 100
@PRC_chinese_sweep_SUBTRACT_VALUE = 25 

PRC_dcat_sweep_commie_cell = {
	PRC_sweep_prc_cell = {
		icon = generic_scorched_earth
		
		highlight_states = {
			state = FROM
		}
		
		state_target = yes
		
		target_array = global.KMT_greater_china_region_states
		
		visible = {
			controls_state = FROM
			FROM = {
				has_state_flag = KMT_PRC_state_has_guerrilla_cell
			}
		}
		
		available = {
			FROM = {
				controller = { tag = ROOT }
			}
			OR = {
				has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > @PRC_chinese_sweep_EQ_COST_TRIGGER }
				is_ai = yes
				divisions_in_state = {
					state = FROM
					size > 0
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			base = @PRC_chinese_sweep_CELL_AI_BASE_FACTOR
			modifier = {
				add = FROM.PRC_state_guerrilla_cell_strength
				FROM = { has_state_flag = KMT_PRC_state_has_guerrilla_cell }
			}
			modifier = {
				is_chinese_nations_w_HYQ = yes
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = communism
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				is_chinese_nations_w_HYQ = no
				NOT = { has_war_with = PRC }
				factor = 0
			}
		}

		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 0

		cost = @PRC_chinese_sweep_CELL_DECISIONS_COST
		
		modifier = {
		}
		
		cancel_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						controller = { tag = ROOT }
					}
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = KMT_PRC_state_has_guerrilla_cell
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = @PRC_chinese_sweep_EQ_COST_EFFECT }
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				FROM = {
					save_global_event_target_as = PRC_temp_sweep_decision_target_state
				}
				set_temp_variable = { var = PRC_chinese_sweep_subtract_value value = @PRC_chinese_sweep_SUBTRACT_VALUE }
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_flag = KMT_PRC_state_has_guerrilla_cell
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = PRC_state_guerrilla_cell_strength value = PRC_chinese_sweep_subtract_value }
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { PRC_state_guerrilla_cell_strength < 1 }
							}
							clr_state_flag = KMT_PRC_state_has_guerrilla_cell
						}
					}
					PRC = { country_event = { id = prc.160 }}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_chinese_sweep_target_state_cell_tt
		}
	}
